Why not use linear regression to this kind of problem? ^yp9oFj8f

y ^aeDgxy6A

x ^dArAnOVa

The case above, with a really simple dataset, if you threshold with 0.5, LR can work, but just with a new example you end up with a really different decision boundary.
So LR is not a good algorithm to classification. ^hpQkFMCs

1 ^Q0h43IsD

Logistic regression ^M25Q2Xu8

By far, the most commonly used classification algorithm is ^siMkUtft

"sigmoid" or "logistic" function ^btNGdXQ2
